style=\"caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">一块极品沉香香料中，只有一小部分才能称得上是奇楠，珍贵难得。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">极品奇楠，历来为皇家贵族所垄断，故一直被称为皇室珍品。</span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" 54);\">奇楠香的成因与普通沉香相同，但两者的性状特佂又有很多差异，所以习惯上让它单成一类，且列为沉香中的极品。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">沉香大都质地坚硬，奇楠则较为柔软，有黏性，削下的碎片甚至能捏成团。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">奇楠香的油脂含量高于沉香，香气也更为甘甜，浓郁。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial style=\"margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">奇楠是沉香中的异种，它在常温下即可自然发香，扩香性好。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">奇楠带明显幽凉花香韵，甘甜优雅，透窍怡人，舒缓心神，堪比天然香水，是上佳的手串原料。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">手串是日常佩戴盘玩之物，用奇楠制作，古朴清雅，香韵长伴。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 25px 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: justify;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">意思就是要积三辈子的德，才有机会闻到奇楠香，足见其难得。</span></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif normal;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><strong><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(67, 87, 143);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">此次众筹的绿奇楠沉香手串原料，就来自于莞香系的主要产区——海南。</span></strong></p><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(54, 54, 54);font-size: 15px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">惠安系：越南及柬埔寨、老挝、泰国、缅甸各地所产沉香，过去因为集中在惠安交易，统称为惠安系。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(54, 54, 54);font-size: 15px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">星洲系：星洲系产地主要在马来西亚﹙东马、西马、文莱﹚、印度尼西亚，过去因集中在新加坡买卖，统称为星洲系。</span></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(54, 54, 54);font-size: 15px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">莞香系：海南、广东、广西。过去因集中在广东东莞买卖，统称为莞香系。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 25px 8px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;text-align: justify;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.4661417322834647\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"635\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; width: 635px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/ibneZHWsor9celY2P6ykbWHfnZzRzjLPg7C971L6ibnEV7LAHuLaRAzh1icCU3hstYpebxFjgLicaJfTSmjpa79BsQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">沉香的形成，可以分为两大类：天然结香和人工结香。<br></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: left;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">天然结香，是指沉香树在特定自然条件下，受伤后被真菌所感染，分泌出油脂后才能形成香脂，这个过程需要数十年甚至上百年的时间。<br></span></p><section style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify border-box break-word><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: left;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">人工结香，是指在健康的沉香树上，人为地制造出结香所需要的外部条件，使沉香树结香。</span></section><section style=\"margin: 25px 8px 10px;text-align: justify;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"387\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"width: 578px; height: 434px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd025wI9FXABOzvZmGg2Uzucib8MRMs6UwQ7iccibic5nXKpThyrhPicjn99hUA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 8px 20px;text-align: right;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><span style=\"color: rgb(84, 84, 84);font-size: 13px;\">野生奇楠树</span></section><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">我国很早就将沉香树列为国家二级保护植物和国际保护树种，禁止砍伐和出口。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">白木香树，就是国家二级保护濒危树种。历史上备受推崇的海南沉香，属于白木香科。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">因为沉香的野生资源难得，一块野生奇楠，价值上千万。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"434\" data-ratio=\"0.6689453125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1024\" style=\"width: 578px; height: 387px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02YhdicfcbE3C0jlPjSiaOkA6qhCdWauYbJMLyjJmKWaLlfXxBPdpdiatKw/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><section style=\"margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">近年来，有香农通过嫁接的方法，成功培育出初代奇楠种苗。</span></section><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">这种可以保留野生奇楠特性的初代奇楠种苗，数年内就可以结出奇楠沉香。</span></p><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">经由野生奇楠树枝桠嫁接的初代绿奇楠，最大程度保留了野生奇楠的香韵与特点。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02gF9bBWrNP1icMXT7yZwSu0nLj4icSIVMVEpLsWR9xnGbn93gic2NuAzKw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">嫁接奇楠苗所结出来的香，经过许多行内爱香专业人士的品鉴，符合市场上所认定的奇楠的特征：</span></section><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">油脂含量高而密度大，油线粗且糖化高、纹路清晰可见；常温下清闻香气十足，奇楠气味明显，有典型的奶香、甜香。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02cc53mahibWqPq7SZjAnWJuwfxbvibb0HbmUibjINosURuaINiarIiaN40SA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">历经嫁接、培育、成材、结香、斫香、勾香、理香，精心挑选结油好，色泽均匀的每一块香材，再打磨加工成大小一致的桶珠或者圆珠。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 25px 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: justify;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"434\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"height: 433px; width: 578px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02qqZIEGTdJibiaSD9q1lWKzGDIoav6AfcN89Cia3adrS3hxLmdgFksjjIw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"color: rgb(54, 54, 54);font-size: 15px;caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif>定制加工的桶珠或者圆珠，比之随形珠，更耗料，需要勾去木质部分，将其粗切成直径一致的香材，再修整打磨。</span></p><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"1.3328125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02wH0dcTDEuTDImjDatfWicCsYfYYl1sHO6Wo8SKoiafY9PTPTpIQLia85w/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">用海南绿奇楠沉香制作的手串，珠粒匀称，大小相若，气韵凝练，质地润泽。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">油脂凝结厚重，呈黄棕色带黑绿色，可见大量深浅不一的褐色油脂条，气味怡人。</span></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\"><span style=\"font-size: 15px;caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);\">因为奇楠油脂含量较普通沉香更高，所以</span>手捏串珠表面，能感受到明显的软润黏手感。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.75\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02bZia7nD2n2CdibHZk2uKWInnCyj0vwcuLwHo2a1bWfjbqPAA0Mj6ghbw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><section style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px 20px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">上等的奇楠香研磨以后，气味芬芳，清凉甘甜，其香能通窍，清爽舒适，即是所谓的“气甜”。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);text-align: left;font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">奇楠粉可以直接入口。嚼之，有嚼蜡或糖的口感，粘牙有黏性，带辛辣麻感并且于口腔留香明显。</span></p><section style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">而嚼普通沉香如同嚼木，无论在口腔中停留多长时间，其木质纤维都不能化开。</span></section><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-cropselx1=\"0\" data-cropselx2=\"578\" data-cropsely1=\"0\" data-cropsely2=\"434\" data-ratio=\"1.3328125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"text-align: center; width: 578px; height: 770px; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/ibneZHWsor9flib6gEh8oRNgqsOINuAd02ylQYlHo9ib1QAqS33P8KsG6OS9rkztqqibyTVR0O92JXLpIogM9asqYQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"caret-color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">由于野生母树数量极少，属于不可再生资源，所以用初代嫁接奇楠制作的沉香手串，也具有良好收藏于佩戴价值，而且更有高性价比，可以说是香友的福音。</span></p><section style=\"margin-bottom: 5px;white-space: normal;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, rgb(54, 54, 54);\">纯银“富甲天下”背云：背云，又名背鱼儿，是佛珠手串上的常见装饰品。“富甲天下”的造型是小龟甲，外形精致可爱。</span></p><p style=\"font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">龟是四灵兽之一，代表长寿吉祥，吉祥富贵。背云名为富甲天下，取囊括天下财富的含义，寓意富贵钱财用之不尽。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 20px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">凉山南红平安扣：<span style=\"font-size: 15px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">凉山南红完整度高、浑厚度好，是目前主流南红矿口。</span></span></p><section style=\"margin: 20px 8px 25px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei arial sans-serif justify><span style=\"font-size: 15px;color: rgb(54, 54, 54);\">南红有鸿运祥瑞的美好寓意，平安扣又寓意“平安”，红色旺运，圆形旺财，南红平安扣融合两者美好寓意，更是吉上添吉。</span></section><p style=\"text-align: justify;margin: 25px 8px;font-family: \" helvetica neue sans gb yahei
